  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.87.0
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/home/cc/.cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/home/cc/.rustup
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/.cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      clang \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      libgit2-dev \
      libgtk-3-dev \
      libxcb-render0-dev \
      libxcb-shape0-dev \
      libxcb-xfixes0-dev \
      libwayland-dev \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      sudo \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      wine64 \
      qemu-user-static \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN mkdir -p /etc/apt/keyrings && \
      curl -fsSL https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu/gpg | gpg --dearmor -o /etc/apt/keyrings/docker.gpg && \
      echo "deb [arch=$(dpkg --print-architecture) signed-by=/etc/apt/keyrings/docker.gpg] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu $(lsb_release -cs) stable" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker.list > /dev/null && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io docker-buildx-plugin docker-compose-plugin && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash cc && \
      usermod -aG sudo,docker cc && \
      echo 'cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL' >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain none && \
      . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustup toolchain install $RUST_VERSION && \
      rustup default $RUST_VERSION && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-docs && \
      rustup target add aarch64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup target add aarch64-unknown-linux-musl && \
      rustup target add x86_64-pc-windows-gnu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cross --git https://github.com/cross-rs/cross && \
      cargo install cargo-binstall && \
      cargo install cargo-audit && \
      cargo install cargo-outdated
  RUN wget -qO- https://github.com/rui314/mold/releases/latest/download/mold-$(uname -m)-linux.tar.gz | tar xz && \
      sudo mv mold*/bin/mold /usr/local/bin/ && \
      sudo chmod +x /usr/local/bin/mold && \
      rm -rf mold*
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data
  RUN git clone https://github.com/nushell/nushell.git nushell_nushell
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nushell_nushell
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked && \
      cargo build --release --features full --locked && \
      cargo build --release --no-default-features --locked && \
      cargo build --release --features static-link-openssl --locked
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cross build --target aarch64-unknown-linux-gnu --release --locked && \
      cross build --target aarch64-unknown-linux-musl --release --features=static-link-openssl --locked
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --workspace --features plugin --locked && \
      cargo test --workspace --locked && \
      cargo test --workspace --features full --locked
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/.config/nushell && \
      ./target/release/nu -c "exit"
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/.cargo && \
      echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "clang"\nrustflags = ["-C", "link-arg=-fuse-ld=/usr/local/bin/mold"]' > /home/cc/.cargo/config.toml.local
  RUN mkdir -p scripts && \
      echo '#!/usr/bin/env nu\n# Build for ARM64 GNU\ncross build --target aarch64-unknown-linux-gnu --release --locked\n# Build for ARM64 musl with static OpenSSL\ncross build --target aarch64-unknown-linux-musl --release --features=static-link-openssl --locked\n# Build for Windows\ncross build --target x86_64-pc-windows-gnu --release --locked' > scripts/cross-build.nu && \
      echo '#!/usr/bin/env nu\ncargo verify-project\ncargo check --locked\ncargo audit\ncargo outdated' > scripts/check-deps.nu && \
      echo '#!/usr/bin/env nu\n# Test stack-intensive operations\nlet large_data = 1..1000000 | each { |i| { index: $i, data: ($i * $i) } }\n$large_data | where index > 500000 | length' > scripts/test-stack-size.nu && \
      chmod +x scripts/*.nu
  RUN echo "/home/cc/.cargo/bin/nu" | sudo tee -a /etc/shells
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install zoxide starship atuin
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --package nu_plugin_example --locked && \
      ./target/release/nu -c "plugin add ./target/debug/nu_plugin_example"
  ENV RUST_BACKTRACE=1
  ENV CARGO_INCREMENTAL=1
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/EnvGym/data/nushell_nushell/target/release:$PATH
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      echo "deb [arch=$(dpkg --print-architecture) signed-by=/etc/apt/keyrings/docker.gpg] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu $(lsb_release -cs) stable" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker.list > /dev/null && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io docker-buildx-plugin docker-compose-plugin && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

      usermod -aG sudo,docker cc && \
      echo 'cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL' >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain none && \
      . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustup toolchain install $RUST_VERSION && \
      rustup default $RUST_VERSION && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-docs && \
      rustup target add aarch64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup target add aarch64-unknown-linux-musl && \
      rustup target add x86_64-pc-windows-gnu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cross --git https://github.com/cross-rs/cross --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cargo-binstall --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cargo-audit --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cargo-outdated --locked || true
  RUN wget -qO- https://github.com/rui314/mold/releases/latest/download/mold-$(uname -m)-linux.tar.gz | tar xz && \

      rm -rf mold*

  WORKDIR /home/cc/nushell_nushell
  COPY --chown=cc:cc . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --features full --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --no-default-features --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --features static-link-openssl --locked || true
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/.config/nushell && \

  RUN echo "/home/cc/.cargo/bin/nu" | sudo tee -a /etc/shells
  ENV RUST_BACKTRACE=1

  FROM ubuntu:20.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV RUST_VERSION=1.87.0
  ENV CARGO_HOME=/home/cc/.cargo
  ENV RUSTUP_HOME=/home/cc/.rustup
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/.cargo/bin:$PATH
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      perl \
      clang \
      libsqlite3-dev \
      libgit2-dev \
      libgtk-3-dev \
      libxcb-render0-dev \
      libxcb-shape0-dev \
      libxcb-xfixes0-dev \
      libwayland-dev \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      sudo \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      wine64 \
      qemu-user-static \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN mkdir -p /etc/apt/keyrings && \
      curl -fsSL https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu/gpg | gpg --dearmor -o /etc/apt/keyrings/docker.gpg && \
      echo "deb [arch=$(dpkg --print-architecture) signed-by=/etc/apt/keyrings/docker.gpg] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu $(lsb_release -cs) stable" | tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker.list > /dev/null && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io docker-buildx-plugin docker-compose-plugin && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash cc && \
      usermod -aG sudo,docker cc && \
      echo 'cc ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL' >> /etc/sudoers
  USER cc
  WORKDIR /home/cc
  RUN curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain none && \
      . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      rustup toolchain install $RUST_VERSION && \
      rustup default $RUST_VERSION && \
      rustup component add rustfmt clippy rust-docs && \
      rustup target add aarch64-unknown-linux-gnu && \
      rustup target add aarch64-unknown-linux-musl && \
      rustup target add x86_64-pc-windows-gnu
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cross --git https://github.com/cross-rs/cross --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cargo-binstall --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cargo-audit --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo install cargo-outdated --locked || true
  RUN for i in 1 2 3; do \
          wget -qO- https://github.com/rui314/mold/releases/download/v2.4.0/mold-2.4.0-$(uname -m)-linux.tar.gz | tar xz && \
          sudo mv mold*/bin/mold /usr/local/bin/ && \
          sudo chmod +x /usr/local/bin/mold && \
          rm -rf mold* && \
          break || \
          if [ $i -eq 3 ]; then echo "Mold installation failed after 3 attempts, continuing without it"; fi; \
          sleep 5; \
      done
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/nushell_nushell
  WORKDIR /home/cc/nushell_nushell
  COPY --chown=cc:cc . .
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --locked
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --features full --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --no-default-features --locked || true
  RUN . $CARGO_HOME/env && \
      cargo build --release --features static-link-openssl --locked || true
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/.config/nushell && \
      ./target/release/nu -c "exit" || true
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/.cargo && \
      if [ -f /usr/local/bin/mold ]; then \
          echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "clang"\nrustflags = ["-C", "link-arg=-fuse-ld=/usr/local/bin/mold"]' > /home/cc/.cargo/config.toml; \
      else \
          echo '[target.x86_64-unknown-linux-gnu]\nlinker = "clang"' > /home/cc/.cargo/config.toml; \
      fi
  RUN echo "/home/cc/.cargo/bin/nu" | sudo tee -a /etc/shells
  ENV RUST_BACKTRACE=1
  ENV CARGO_INCREMENTAL=1
  ENV PATH=/home/cc/nushell_nushell/target/release:$PATH
  WORKDIR /home/cc/nushell_nushell
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
